Maternal Serum Analyte Screening includes a two part blood draw (+/- nuchal cord translucency) done at specific times of the pregnancy, that looks at proteins associated with this pregnancy. By analyzing the proteins and their ratios, the test will give a personal risk ratio rather than an age risk ratio. Our goal is to identify pts. that have a higher chance of having a baby with DS, T18, or NT Defects, in order to adjust her pregnancy including additional tests, monitoring frequency and to prepare families. If the test comes back positive, the baby can be normal but this can cause a lot of stress. It can also come back low risk and the baby of Down syndrome.
